   śrīgaruḍamahāpurāṇam	SrI garuxa mahApurANam
   śrīgaṇeśāyanamaḥ /	SrI gaNeSAya namaH /
   śrīlakṣmīnṛsiṃhāya namaḥ /	SrI lakzmI nRsiMhAya namaH /
   śrīdattātreyāya namaḥ /	SrIdattAtreyAya namaH /
   śrīvedavyāsāya namaḥ /	SrI vedavyAsAya namaH /
   śrīhayagrīvāya namaḥ /	SrI hayagrIvAya namaH /
   atha gāruḍe brahmakāṇḍastṛtīya ārabhyate /	aTa gAruxe brahmakANxaH tRtIyaH AraByate /
   oṃ mallānāmaśanirnṛṇāṃ naravaraḥ strīṇāṃ smaro mūrtimān gopānāṃ svajano	om mallAnAm aSaniH nRNAm nara varaH strINAm smaraH mUrtimAn gopAnAm sva janaH 
   'satāṃ kṣitibhṛtāṃ śāstā svapitroḥ śiśuḥ /	asatAm kzitiBRtAm SAstA sva pitroH SiSuH /
   mṛtyurbhojapatervidhātṛvihita stattvaṃ paraṃ yogināṃ vṛṣṇīnāṃ ca patiḥ	mRtyuH BojapateH viDAtR vihita stattvam param yoginAm vRzNInAm ca patiH
   sadaiva śuśubhe raṅge 'cyutaḥ sāgrajaḥ // GarP_3,1.1 //	sadA eva SuSuBe raFge acyutaH sAgrajaH // GarP_3,1.1 //
   namo nārāyaṇāyeti tasmai vai mūlarūpiṇe /	namaH nArAyaNAya iti tasmE vE mUla rUpiNe /
   namaskṛtya pravakṣyāmi nārāyaṇakathāmimām // GarP_3,1.2 //	namaskRtya pravakzyAmi nArAyaNa kaTAm imAm // GarP_3,1.2 //
   śaunakādyā mahātmāno hyṛṣayo brahmavādinaḥ /	SOnaka AdyAH mahAtmAnaH hi RzayaH brahma vAdinaH /
   naimiṣākhye mahāpuṇye tapastepurmahattaram // GarP_3,1.3 //	nEmiza AKye mahA puNye tapaH tepuH mahattaram // GarP_3,1.3 //
   jitendriyā jitāhārāḥ saṃtaḥ satyaparāyaṇāḥ /	jita indriyAH jita AhArAH saMtaH satya parAyaNAH /
   yajantaḥ parayā bhaktyā viṣṇumādyaṃ jagadgurum // GarP_3,1.4 //	yajantaH parayA BaktyA vizNum Adyam jagadgurum // GarP_3,1.4 //
   gṛṇantaḥ paramaṃ brahma jagaccakṣurmahaujasaḥ /	gRNantaH paramam brahma jagaccakzuH mahA ojasaH /
   sarvaśāstrārthatattvajñāstepurnaimiṣa kānane // GarP_3,1.5 //	sarva SAstra arTa tattva jQAH tepuH nEmiza kAnane // GarP_3,1.5 //
   yajñairyajñapatiṃ kecijjñānairjñānātmakaṃ param /	yajQEH yajQa patim kecid jQAnEH jQAna Atmakam param /
   kecitparamayā bhaktyā nārāyaṇamapūjayan // GarP_3,1.6 //	kecid paramayA BaktyA nArAyaNam apUjayan // GarP_3,1.6 //
   ekadā tu mahātmānaḥ samājaṃ cakruruttamāḥ /	ekadA tu mahAtmAnaH samAjam cakruH uttamAH /
   dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇāmupāyaṃ jñātumicchavaḥ // GarP_3,1.7 //	Darma arTa kAma mokzANAm upAyam jQAtum icCavaH // GarP_3,1.7 //
   ṣadviṃśatisahasrāṇi munīnāmūrdhvaretasām /	zad viMSati sahasrANi munInAm UrDvaretasAm /
   teṣāṃ śiṣyapraśiṣyāṇāṃ saṃkhyā vaktuṃ na śaṅkyate // GarP_3,1.8 //	tezAm Sizya praSizyANAm saMKyA vaktum na SaFkyate // GarP_3,1.8 //
   munayo bhāvitātmāno militāste mahojasaḥ /	munayaH BAvitAtmAnaH militAH te mahojasaH /
   lokānugrahakartāro vītarāgā vimatsarāḥ // GarP_3,1.9 //	loka anugraha kartAraH vIta rAgAH vimatsarAH // GarP_3,1.9 //
   kathaṃ harau manuṣyāṇāṃ bhaktiravyabhicāriṇī /	kaTam harO manuzyANAm BaktiH avyaBicAriNI /
   kena sidhyettu sakalaṃ karma trividhamātmanaḥ // GarP_3,1.10 //	kena siDyet tu sakalam karma triviDam AtmanaH // GarP_3,1.10 //
   ityevaṃ praṣṭumātmānamudyatānprekṣya śaunakaḥ /	iti evam prazwum AtmAnam udyatAn prekzya SOnakaH /
   sāṃja lirvākyamāha sma vinayāvanataḥ sudhīḥ // GarP_3,1.11 //	sAMja liH vAkyam Aha sma vinaya avanataH suDIH // GarP_3,1.11 //
   śaunaka uvāca /	SOnakaH uvAca /
   āste siddhāśrame puṇye sūtaḥ paurāṇikottamaḥ /	Aste sidDASrame puNye sUtaH pOrANika uttamaH /
   sa etadakhilaṃ vetti vyāsaśiṣyo yatīśvaraḥ // GarP_3,1.12 //	saH etat aKilam vetti vyAsa SizyaH yati ISvaraH // GarP_3,1.12 //
   tasmāttameva pṛcchāma ityevaṃ śaunako muniḥ /	tasmAt tam eva pRcCAmaH iti evam SOnakaH muniH /
   atha te ṛṣayo jagmuḥ puṇyaṃ siddhāśramaṃ tataḥ // GarP_3,1.13 //	aTa te RzayaH jagmuH puNyam sidDASramam tatas // GarP_3,1.13 //
   papracchuste sukhāsīnaṃ naimiṣāraṇyavāsinaḥ /	papracCuH te suKa AsInam nEmiza araNya vAsinaH /
   ṛṣaya ūcuḥ /	RzayaH UcuH /
   vayaṃ tvatithayaḥ prāptāstvātitheyosi suvrata // GarP_3,1.14 //	vayam tu atiTayaH prAptAH tu AtiTeyosi suvrata // GarP_3,1.14 //
   snānadānopacāreṇa pūjayitvā yathāvidhi /	snAna dAna upacAreNa pUjayitvA yaTAviDi /
   kena viṣṇuḥ prasannaḥ syātsa kathaṃ pūjyate naraiḥ // GarP_3,1.15 //	kena vizNuH prasannaH syAt sa kaTam pUjyate narEH // GarP_3,1.15 //
   muktisādhanabhūtaṃ ca brūhi tattvavinirṇayam /	mukti sADana BUtam ca brUhi tattva vinirNayam /
   sūta uvāca /	sUtaH uvAca /
   śṛṇudhvamṛṣyaḥ sarve hariṃ tattvavinirṇayam // GarP_3,1.16 //	SRNuDvam RzyaH sarve harim tattva vinirNayam // GarP_3,1.16 //
   natvā viṣṇuṃ śriyaṃ vāyuṃ bhāratīṃ śeṣasaṃjñakam /	natvA vizNum Sriyam vAyum BAratIm Seza saMjQakam /
   dvaipāyanaṃ guruṃ kṛṣṇaṃ pravakṣyāmi yathāmati // GarP_3,1.17 //	dvEpAyanam gurum kRzNam pravakzyAmi yaTAmati // GarP_3,1.17 //
   nāsti nārāyaṇasamaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati /	na asti nArAyaNa samam na BUtam na Bavizyati /
   etena satyavākyena sarvārthānsādhayāmyaham // GarP_3,1.18 //	etena satya vAkyena sarva arTAn sADayAmi aham // GarP_3,1.18 //
   śaunaka uvāca /	SOnakaH uvAca /
   kimarthaṃ namanaṃ viṣṇorgranthādau munisattama /	kimarTam namanam vizNoH granTa AdO muni sattamaH /
   kartavyaṃ brūhi me brahmankṛpayā mama suvrata // GarP_3,1.19 //	kartavyam brUhi me brahman kRpayA mama suvrata // GarP_3,1.19 //
   tataḥ śriyaṃ tato vāyuṃ bhāratīṃ ca tataḥ param /	tatas Sriyam tatas vAyum BAratIm ca tatas param /
   ante vyāsaṃ kimarthaṃ ca tvaṃ namaskṛtavānasi /	ante vyAsam kim arTam ca tvam namaskRtavAn asi /
   sūtasūta mahābhāga brūhi kāraṇamatra ca // GarP_3,1.20 //	sUtasUta mahABAga brUhi kAraNam atra ca // GarP_3,1.20 //
   sūta uvāca /	sUtaH uvAca /
   ādau vandyaḥ sarvavedaikavedyo vede śāstre setihāse purāṇe /	AdO vandyaH sarva veda eka vedyaH vede SAstre sa itihAse purANe /
   sattāṃ prāyo viṣṇurevaika eva prakāśate 'to namya eko harirhi //	sattAm prAyas vizNuH eva ekaH eva prakASate atas namyaH ekaH hariH hi //
   GarP_3,1.21 //	GarP_3,1.21 //
   sarvatra mukhyastvadhikonyatopi sa eva namyo na ca śaṅkarādyāḥ /	sarvatra muKyaH tu aDikonyatopi saH eva namyaH na ca SaFkara AdyAH /
   namanti ye 'vinayācchaṅkaraṃ tu vināyakaṃ caṇḍikāṃ reṇukāṃ ca //	namanti ye avinayAt SaFkaram tu vinAyakam caNxikAm reNukAm ca //
   GarP_3,1.22 //	GarP_3,1.22 //
   tathā sūryaṃ bhairavaṃ mātāraśva tathā vāṇīṃ girijāṃ vai śriyaṃ ca /	taTA sUryam BEravam mAtAraSva taTA vANIm girijAm vE Sriyam ca /
   sarvepi te vaiṣṇavā naiva loke na tadbhaktā veti cāryā vadanti //	sarvepi te vEzNavAH na eva loke na tad BaktA vA iti ca AryAH vadanti //
   GarP_3,1.23 //	GarP_3,1.23 //
   na pārthikyānnamanaṃ kāryameva prīṇanti naitā devatāḥ pūjanena /	na pArTikyAt namanam kAryam eva prINanti na etAH devatAH pUjanena /
   pūjāṃ gṛhītvā devatāścaiva sarvāḥ kiñciddatvā phaladānena tāṃśca //	pUjAm gRhItvA devatAH ca eva sarvAH kiQcid datvA Pala dAnena tAn= ca //
   GarP_3,1.24 //	GarP_3,1.24 //
   saṃtarpya tuṣṭaiḥ svamanonu sārāttaiḥ kāritāṃ kāmyapūjāṃ tathaiva /	saMtarpya tuzwEH sva manonu sArAttEH kAritAm kAmya pUjAm taTA eva /
   nivedayitvā paradevatāyāṃ viṣṇau harau śrīpuruṣādivandye // GarP_3,1.25 //	nivedayitvA para devatAyAm vizNO harO SrI puruza Adi vandye // GarP_3,1.25 //
   ihāparatrāpi sukhetarāṇi dāsyanti paścādadharaṃ vai tamaśca /	iha aparatra api suKa itarANi dAsyanti paScAt aDaram vE tamaH ca /
   ato hyete naiva pūjyā na namyā mokṣecchubhirbrāhmaṇādyairdvijendra //	atas hi ete na eva pUjyAH na namyAH mokza it SuBiH brAhmaNa AdyEH dvija indra //
   GarP_3,1.26 //	GarP_3,1.26 //
   tathaiva sarvāśramibhiśca nityaṃ mahāvipattāvapi vipravaryāḥ /	taTA eva sarva ASramiBiH ca nityam mahA vipattO= api vipra varyAH /
   śrīkāmya yā ye tu bhajanti nityaṃ śrībrahmarudredrayamādidevān //	SrI kAmya yAH ye tu Bajanti nityam SrI brahma rudredrayam AdidevAn //
   GarP_3,1.27 //	GarP_3,1.27 //
   iheva bhuñjanti mahacca duḥ khaṃ mahāpadaḥ kuṣṭhabhagandarādīn /	iha iva BuQjanti mahat ca duH Kam mahApadaH kuzWa Bagandara AdIn /
   namanti ye 'vaiṣṇavānbrahmarudravāyu pratīkānnaiva te viṣṇubhaktāḥ //	namanti ye avEzNavAn brahma rudra vAyu pratIkAt na eva te vizNu BaktAH //
   GarP_3,1.28 //	GarP_3,1.28 //
   abhiprāyaṃ tvatra vakṣye munīndrāḥ paraṃ gopyaṃ hṛdi dhāryaṃ hi taddhi /	aBiprAyam tu atra vakzye muni indrAH param gopyam hRdi DAryam hi tat hi /
   vāyoḥ pratīkaṃ pūjyameveha viprā na brahmarudrādipratīkameva //	vAyoH pratIkam pUjyam eva iha viprAH na brahmarudra Adi pratIkam eva //
   GarP_3,1.29 //	GarP_3,1.29 //
   pūjākāle devadevasya viṣṇorvāyoḥ pratīkaṃ yogyabhāge nidhāya /	pUjA kAle devadevasya vizNoH vAyoH pratIkam yogya BAge niDAya /
   antargataṃ tasya vāyorhariṃ ca lakṣmīpatiṃ pūjayitvā hi samyak //	antargatam tasya vAyoH harim ca lakzmIpatim pUjayitvA hi samyak //
   GarP_3,1.30 //	GarP_3,1.30 //
   paścādvāyoḥ supratīkaṃ ca samyaṅ nirmālyaśeṣeṇa hareḥ samarcayet /	paScAt vAyoH supratIkam ca samyak nirmAlya SezeNa hareH samarcayet /
   pṛthakca sragdhūpavilepanādipūjāṃ prakurvanti ca ye vimūḍhaḥ //	pRTak ca sraj DUpa vilepana Adi pUjAm prakurvanti ca ye vimUXaH //
   GarP_3,1.31 //	GarP_3,1.31 //
   teṣāṃ duḥ khamiha loke paratra bhaviṣyate nātra vicāryamasti /	tezAm duH Kam iha loke paratra Bavizyate na atra vicAryam asti /
   prāyaścittaṃ svasti viprāḥ kathañcittatkurvantu smaraṇaṃ nāma viṣṇoḥ //	prAyaScittam svasti viprAH kaTaQcid tat kurvantu smaraNam nAma vizNoH //
   GarP_3,1.32 //	GarP_3,1.32 //
   pāṣaṇḍarudrādikasaṃ pratiṣṭhitānharervāyoḥ śaṅkarasya pratīkān /	pAzaNxa rudra Adi kasam pratizWitAn hareH vAyoH SaFkarasya pratIkAn /
   namanti ye phalabuddhyā vibhūḍhāsteṣāṃ phalaṃ śāśvataṃ duḥ khameva //	namanti ye Pala budDyA viBUXAH tezAm Palam SASvatam duH Kam eva //
   GarP_3,1.33 //	GarP_3,1.33 //
   vāyoḥ pratīkaṃ yadi vipravaryaiḥ pratiṣṭhitaṃ cennamanaṃ hi kāryam /	vAyoH pratIkam yadi vipra varyEH pratizWitam ced namanam hi kAryam /
   naivedyaśeṣeṇa hareśca viṣṇoḥ pūjā kṛtā cenna hi doṣaleśaḥ // GarP_3,1.34	nEvedya SezeNa hareH ca vizNoH pUjA kRtA ced na hi doza leSaH // GarP_3,1.34
   gururhi mukhyo hanumajjanirmahānrāmāṅghribhakto hanumānsadaiva /	guruH hi muKyaH hanu majja niH mahAn rAma aFGri BaktaH hanumAn sadA eva /
   evaṃ viditvā paramaṃ hariṃ ca putraṃ punarmukhyadevasya vāyoḥ //	evam viditvA paramam harim ca putram punar muKya devasya vAyoH //
   GarP_3,1.35 //	GarP_3,1.35 //
   namaskāro nānyathā vipravaryā ādhīyatāṃ hṛdi sarvai rahasyamam /	namaskAraH na anyaTA vipra varyAH ADIyatAm hRdi sarvEH rahasyamam /
   ye vaiṣṇavā vaiṣṇa vadāsabhṛtyāḥ sarvepi te sarvadā viṣṇumeva //	ye vEzNavAH vEzNa vadAsa BRtyAH sarva ipi te sarvadA vizNum eva //
   GarP_3,1.36 /	GarP_3,1.36 /
   namanti ye vai pratipādayanti tathaiva puṇyāni ca sāttvikāni /	namanti ye vE pratipAdayanti taTA eva puNyAni ca sAttvikAni /
   namanti ye vāsudevaṃ hariṃ ca samyak svaśaktyā pratipādayanti //	namanti ye vAsudevam harim ca samyak sva SaktyA pratipAdayanti //
   GarP_3,1.37 //	GarP_3,1.37 //
   pravṛttimārgeṇa na pūjayanti hyāpatkāle paradaivaṃ tadanyam /	pravRtti mArgeNa na pUjayanti hi Apad kAle para dEvam tad anyam /
   te vaiṣṇavā vaiṣṇavadāsabhṛtyā anye ca sarve 'vaiṣṇavamātrakāḥ smṛtāḥ //	te vEzNavAH vEzNava dAsa BRtyAH anye ca sarve avEzNava mAtrakAH smRtAH //
   GarP_3,1.38 //	GarP_3,1.38 //
   upakramairupasaṃhārasya liṅgairhariṃ guruṃ hyantareṇaiva yānti /	upakramEH upasaMhArasya liFgEH harim gurum hi antareNa eva yAnti /
   tānevāhuḥ satpurāṇāni viprāḥ kalau yuge nābhyasūyanti sarve // GarP_3,1.39	tAn eva AhuH sat purANAni viprAH kalO yuge na aByasUyanti sarve // GarP_3,1.39
   yato hitānye pratipādayanti pravṛttidharmānsvasvavarṇānurūpān /	yatas hita anye pratipAdayanti pravRtti DarmAn sva sva varNa anurUpAn /
   ato hyasūyanti sadā vimūḍhāḥ kalau hi viprāḥ pracurā hi tepi //	atas hi asUyanti sadA vimUXAH kalO hi viprAH pracurAH hi tepi //
   GarP_3,1.40 //	GarP_3,1.40 //
   na cāsti viṣṇoḥ sadṛśaṃ ca daivataṃ na cāsti vāyoḥ sadṛśo guruśca /	na ca asti vizNoH sadRSam ca dEvatam na ca asti vAyoH sadRSaH guruH ca /
   na cāsti tīrthaṃ sadṛśaṃ viṣṇupadyāḥ na viṣṇubhaktena samosti bhaktaḥ //	na ca asti tIrTam sadRSam vizNupadyAH na vizNu Baktena samosti BaktaH //
   GarP_3,1.41 //	GarP_3,1.41 //
   anyāni viṣṇoḥ pratipādakāni sarvāṇi te sāttvikānīti cāhuḥ /	anyAni vizNoH pratipAdakAni sarvANi te sAttvikAni iti ca AhuH /
   śrāvyāṇi tānyeva manuṣyaloke śrāvyāṇi nānyāni ca duḥ khadāni //	SrAvyANi tAni eva manuzya loke SrAvyANi na anyAni ca duH KadAni //
   GarP_3,1.42 //	GarP_3,1.42 //
   kalau yuge sarva purāṇamadhye trīṇyeva mukhyāni haripriyāṇi /	kalO yuge sarve purANa maDye trINi eva muKyAni hari priyANi /
   mukhyaṃ purāṇaṃ hi kalau nṛṇāṃ ca śreyaskaraṃ bhāgavataṃ purāṇam //	muKyam purANam hi kalO nRNAm ca Sreyaskaram BAgavatam purANam //
   GarP_3,1.43 //	GarP_3,1.43 //
   pūrvaṃ hi sṛṣṭiḥ pratipādyate tra yato hyato bhāgavataṃ paraṃ smṛtam /	pUrvam hi sRzwiH pratipAdyate tra yatas hi atas BAgavatam param smRtam /
   yasminpurāṇe kathayanti sṛṣṭiṃ hyādau viṣṇorbrahmarudrādikānām //	yasmin purANe kaTayanti sRzwim hi AdO vizNoH brahma rudra AdikAnAm //
   GarP_3,1.44 //	GarP_3,1.44 //
   nānārthamevaṃ kathayanti vipra nīcoccarūpaṃ jñānamāhurmahāntaḥ /	nAnA arTam evam kaTayanti vipra nIca ucca rUpam jQAnam AhuH mahAntaH /
   tenaiva siddhaṃ pravadanti sarvaṃ hyataḥ paraṃ bhāgavataṃ purāṇam //	tena eva sidDam pravadanti sarvam hi atas param BAgavatam purANam //
   GarP_3,1.45 //	GarP_3,1.45 //
   tataḥ paraṃ viṣṇupurāṇamāhustataḥ paraṃ gāruḍasaṃjñakaṃ ca /	tatas param vizNupurANam AhuH tatas param gAruxa saMjQakam ca /
   trīṇyeva mukhyā ni kalau nṛṇāṃ tu tathā viśeṣo gāruḍe kiñcidasti //	trINi eva muKyAH ni kalO nRNAm tu taTA viSezaH gAruxe kiQcid asti //
   GarP_3,1.46 //	GarP_3,1.46 //
   śṛṇudhvaṃ vai taṃ viśeṣaṃ ca viprāstryaṃśairyuktaṃ gāruḍākhyaṃ purāṇam /	SRNuDvam vE tam viSezam ca viprAH tri aMSEH yuktam gAruxa AKyam purANam /
   ādyāṃśaṃ vai karmakāṇḍaṃ vadanti dvitīyāṃśaṃ dharmakāṇḍaṃ tamāhuḥ //	Adya aMSam vE karma kANxam vadanti dvitIya aMSam Darma kANxam tam AhuH //
   GarP_3,1.47 //	GarP_3,1.47 //
   tṛtīyāṃśaṃ brahmakāṇḍaṃ vadanti teṣāṃ madhye tvantimoyaṃ variṣṭhaḥ /	tRtIya aMSam brahma kANxam vadanti tezAm maDye tu anti moyam varizWaH /
   tṛtīyāṃśaśravaṇātpuṇyamāhustulyaṃ puṇyaṃ bhāgavatasya viprāḥ //	tRtIya aMSa SravaNAt puNyam AhuH tulyam puNyam BAgavatasya viprAH //
   GarP_3,1.48 //	GarP_3,1.48 //
   tṛtīyāṃśe paṭhite vedatulyaṃ phalaṃ bhavennātra vicāryamasti /	tRtIya aMSe paWite veda tulyam Palam Bavet na atra vicAryam asti /
   tṛtīyāṃśaśravaṇādeva viprāḥ phalaṃ proktaṃ paṭhatopyarthamevam //	tRtIya aMSa SravaNAt eva viprAH Palam proktam paWata upyarTam evam //
   GarP_3,1.49 //	GarP_3,1.49 //

   śrīgaruḍamahāpurāṇam  13	SrI garuxa mahApurANam 13

   medhagaṃbhīrayā vācā provāca madhusūdanaḥ // GarP_3,13.1 //	meDa gaMBIrayA vAcA provAca maDusUdanaH // GarP_3,13.1 //
   sṛja brahmannimāndevānmatprasādātkrameṇa ca /	sRja brahman= imAn devAt mad prasAdAt krameNa ca /

   śrīgaruḍamahāpurāṇam  17	SrI garuxa mahApurANam 17

   ekadeha viśiṣṭaiva bhuvi jāteti coktavān // GarP_3,17.1 //	eka dA iha viSizwA eva Buvi jAtA iti ca uktavAn // GarP_3,17.1 //
